<a name="section-75_p15"></a>**15** And again, I say unto my servant Asa Dodds, and unto my servant Calves Wilson, that they also shall take their journey unto the western countries, and proclaim my gospel, even as I have commanded them.

<a name="section-75_p16"></a>**16** And he who is faithful shall overcome all things, and shall be lifted up at the last day.

<a name="section-75_p17"></a>**17** And again, I say unto my servant Major N. Ashley, and my servant Burr Riggs, let them take their journey also into the south country.

<a name="section-75_p18"></a>**18** Yea, let all those take their journey, as I have commanded them, going from house to house, and from village to village, and from city to city.

<a name="section-75_p19"></a>**19** And in whatsoever house ye enter, and they receive you, leave your blessing upon that house.

<a name="section-75_p20"></a>**20** And in whatsoever house ye enter, and they receive you not, ye shall depart speedily from that house, and shake off the dust of your feet as a testimony against them.

<a name="section-75_p21"></a>**21** And you shall be filled with joy and gladness; and know this, that in the day of judgment you shall be judges of that house, and condemn them;

<a name="section-75_p22"></a>**22** And it shall be more tolerable for the heathen in the day of judgment, than for that house; therefore, gird up your loins and be faithful, and ye shall overcome all things, and be lifted up at the last day. Even so. Amen.

<a name="section-75_p23"></a>**23** And again, thus saith the Lord unto you, O ye elders of my church, who have given your names that you might know his will concerning you—

<a name="section-75_p24"></a>**24** Behold, I say unto you, that it is the duty of the church to assist in supporting the families of those, and also to support the families of those who are called and must needs be sent unto the world to proclaim the gospel unto the world.

<a name="section-75_p25"></a>**25** Wherefore, I, the Lord, give unto you this commandment, that ye obtain places for your families, inasmuch as your brethren are willing to open their hearts.

<a name="section-75_p26"></a>**26** And let all such as can obtain places for their families, and support of the church for them, not fail to go into the world, whether to the east or to the west, or to the north, or to the south.

<a name="section-75_p27"></a>**27** Let them ask and they shall receive, knock and it shall be opened unto them, and be made known from on high, even by the Comforter, whither they shall go.

<a name="section-75_p28"></a>**28** And again, verily I say unto you, that every man who is obliged to provide for his own family, let him provide, and he shall in nowise lose his crown; and let him labor in the church.

<a name="section-75_p29"></a>**29** Let every man be diligent in all things. And the idler shall not have place in the church, except he repent and mend his ways.

<a name="section-75_p30"></a>**30** Wherefore, let my servant Simeon Carter and my servant Emer Harris be united in the ministry;

<a name="section-75_p31"></a>**31** And also my servant Ezra Thayre and my servant Thomas B. Marsh;

<a name="section-75_p32"></a>**32** Also my servant Hyrum Smith and my servant Reynolds Cahoon;

<a name="section-75_p33"></a>**33** And also my servant Daniel Stanton and my servant Seymour Brunson;

<a name="section-75_p34"></a>**34** And also my servant Sylvester Smith and my servant Gideon Carter;

<a name="section-75_p35"></a>**35** And also my servant Ruggles Eames and my servant Stephen Burnett;

<a name="section-75_p36"></a>**36** And also my servant Micah B. Welton and also my servant Eden Smith. Even so. Amen.


---

## <a name="section-76"></a>Section 76

<a name="section-76_p1"></a>**1** Hear, O ye heavens, and give ear, O earth, and rejoice ye inhabitants thereof, for the Lord is God, and beside him there is no Savior.

<a name="section-76_p2"></a>**2** Great is his wisdom, marvelous are his ways, and the extent of his doings none can find out.

<a name="section-76_p3"></a>**3** His purposes fail not, neither are there any who can stay his hand.

<a name="section-76_p4"></a>**4** From eternity to eternity he is the same, and his years never fail.

<a name="section-76_p5"></a>**5** For thus saith the Lord—I, the Lord, am merciful and gracious unto those who fear me, and delight to honor those who serve me in righteousness and in truth unto the end.

<a name="section-76_p6"></a>**6** Great shall be their reward and eternal shall be their glory.

<a name="section-76_p7"></a>**7** And to them will I reveal all mysteries, yea, all the hidden mysteries of my kingdom from days of old, and for ages to come, will I make known unto them the good pleasure of my will concerning all things pertaining to my kingdom.

<a name="section-76_p8"></a>**8** Yea, even the wonders of eternity shall they know, and things to come will I show them, even the things of many generations.

<a name="section-76_p9"></a>**9** And their wisdom shall be great, and their understanding reach to heaven; and before them the wisdom of the wise shall perish, and the understanding of the prudent shall come to naught.

<a name="section-76_p10"></a>**10** For by my Spirit will I enlighten them, and by my power will I make known unto them the secrets of my will—yea, even those things which eye has not seen, nor ear heard, nor yet entered into the heart of man.

<a name="section-76_p11"></a>**11** We, Joseph Smith, Jun., and Sidney Rigdon, being in the Spirit on the sixteenth day of February, in the year of our Lord one thousand eight hundred and thirty-two—

<a name="section-76_p12"></a>**12** By the power of the Spirit our eyes were opened and our understandings were enlightened, so as to see and understand the things of God—

<a name="section-76_p13"></a>**13** Even those things which were from the beginning before the world was, which were ordained of the Father, through his Only Begotten Son, who was in the bosom of the Father, even from the beginning;

<a name="section-76_p14"></a>**14** Of whom we bear record; and the record which we bear is the fulness of the gospel of Jesus Christ, who is the Son, whom we saw and with whom we conversed in the heavenly vision.

<a name="section-76_p15"></a>**15** For while we were doing the work of translation, which the Lord had appointed unto us, we came to the twenty-ninth verse of the fifth chapter of John, which was given unto us as follows—

<a name="section-76_p16"></a>**16** Speaking of the resurrection of the dead, concerning those who shall hear the voice of the Son of Man:

<a name="section-76_p17"></a>**17** And shall come forth; they who have done good, in the resurrection of the just; and they who have done evil, in the resurrection of the unjust.

<a name="section-76_p18"></a>**18** Now this caused us to marvel, for it was given unto us of the Spirit.

<a name="section-76_p19"></a>**19** And while we meditated upon these things, the Lord touched the eyes of our understandings and they were opened, and the glory of the Lord shone round about.

<a name="section-76_p20"></a>**20** And we beheld the glory of the Son, on the right hand of the Father, and received of his fulness;

<a name="section-76_p21"></a>**21** And saw the holy angels, and them who are sanctified before his throne, worshiping God, and the Lamb, who worship him forever and ever.

<a name="section-76_p22"></a>**22** And now, after the many testimonies which have been given of him, this is the testimony, last of all, which we give of him: That he lives!

<a name="section-76_p23"></a>**23** For we saw him, even on the right hand of God; and we heard the voice bearing record that he is the Only Begotten of the Father—

<a name="section-76_p24"></a>**24** That by him, and through him, and of him, the worlds are and were created, and the inhabitants thereof are begotten sons and daughters unto God.

<a name="section-76_p25"></a>**25** And this we saw also, and bear record, that an angel of God who was in authority in the presence of God, who rebelled against the Only Begotten Son whom the Father loved and who was in the bosom of the Father, was thrust down from the presence of God and the Son,

<a name="section-76_p26"></a>**26** And was called Perdition, for the heavens wept over him—he was Lucifer, a son of the morning.

<a name="section-76_p27"></a>**27** And we beheld, and lo, he is fallen! is fallen, even a son of the morning!

<a name="section-76_p28"></a>**28** And while we were yet in the Spirit, the Lord commanded us that we should write the vision; for we beheld Satan, that old serpent, even the devil, who rebelled against God, and sought to take the kingdom of our God and his Christ—

<a name="section-76_p29"></a>**29** Wherefore, he maketh war with the saints of God, and encompasseth them round about.

<a name="section-76_p30"></a>**30** And we saw a vision of the sufferings of those with whom he made war and overcame, for thus came the voice of the Lord unto us:

<a name="section-76_p31"></a>**31** Thus saith the Lord concerning all those who know my power, and have been made partakers thereof, and suffered themselves through the power of the devil to be overcome, and to deny the truth and defy my power—

<a name="section-76_p32"></a>**32** They are they who are the sons of perdition, of whom I say that it had been better for them never to have been born;

<a name="section-76_p33"></a>**33** For they are vessels of wrath, doomed to suffer the wrath of God, with the devil and his angels in eternity;

<a name="section-76_p34"></a>**34** Concerning whom I have said there is no forgiveness in this world nor in the world to come—

<a name="section-76_p35"></a>**35** Having denied the Holy Spirit after having received it, and having denied the Only Begotten Son of the Father, having crucified him unto themselves and put him to an open shame.

<a name="section-76_p36"></a>**36** These are they who shall go away into the lake of fire and brimstone, with the devil and his angels—

<a name="section-76_p37"></a>**37** And the only ones on whom the second death shall have any power;

<a name="section-76_p38"></a>**38** Yea, verily, the only ones who shall not be redeemed in the due time of the Lord, after the sufferings of his wrath.

<a name="section-76_p39"></a>**39** For all the rest shall be brought forth by the resurrection of the dead, through the triumph and the glory of the Lamb, who was slain, who was in the bosom of the Father before the worlds were made.

<a name="section-76_p40"></a>**40** And this is the gospel, the glad tidings, which the voice out of the heavens bore record unto us—

<a name="section-76_p41"></a>**41** That he came into the world, even Jesus, to be crucified for the world, and to bear the sins of the world, and to sanctify the world, and to cleanse it from all unrighteousness;

<a name="section-76_p42"></a>**42** That through him all might be saved whom the Father had put into his power and made by him;

<a name="section-76_p43"></a>**43** Who glorifies the Father, and saves all the works of his hands, except those sons of perdition who deny the Son after the Father has revealed him.

<a name="section-76_p44"></a>**44** Wherefore, he saves all except them—they shall go away into everlasting punishment, which is endless punishment, which is eternal punishment, to reign with the devil and his angels in eternity, where their worm dieth not, and the fire is not quenched, which is their torment—

<a name="section-76_p45"></a>**45** And the end thereof, neither the place thereof, nor their torment, no man knows;

<a name="section-76_p46"></a>**46** Neither was it revealed, neither is, neither will be revealed unto man, except to them who are made partakers thereof;

<a name="section-76_p47"></a>**47** Nevertheless, I, the Lord, show it by vision unto many, but straightway shut it up again;

<a name="section-76_p48"></a>**48** Wherefore, the end, the width, the height, the depth, and the misery thereof, they understand not, neither any man except those who are ordained unto this condemnation.

<a name="section-76_p49"></a>**49** And we heard the voice, saying: Write the vision, for lo, this is the end of the vision of the sufferings of the ungodly.

<a name="section-76_p50"></a>**50** And again we bear record—for we saw and heard, and this is the testimony of the gospel of Christ concerning them who shall come forth in the resurrection of the just—

<a name="section-76_p51"></a>**51** They are they who received the testimony of Jesus, and believed on his name and were baptized after the manner of his burial, being buried in the water in his name, and this according to the commandment which he has given—

<a name="section-76_p52"></a>**52** That by keeping the commandments they might be washed and cleansed from all their sins, and receive the Holy Spirit by the laying on of the hands of him who is ordained and sealed unto this power;

<a name="section-76_p53"></a>**53** And who overcome by faith, and are sealed by the Holy Spirit of promise, which the Father sheds forth upon all those who are just and true.

<a name="section-76_p54"></a>**54** They are they who are the church of the Firstborn.

<a name="section-76_p55"></a>**55** They are they into whose hands the Father has given all things—

<a name="section-76_p56"></a>**56** They are they who are priests and kings, who have received of his fulness, and of his glory;

<a name="section-76_p57"></a>**57** And are priests of the Most High, after the order of Melchizedek, which was after the order of Enoch, which was after the order of the Only Begotten Son.

<a name="section-76_p58"></a>**58** Wherefore, as it is written, they are gods, even the sons of God—

<a name="section-76_p59"></a>**59** Wherefore, all things are theirs, whether life or death, or things present, or things to come, all are theirs and they are Christ’s, and Christ is God’s.

<a name="section-76_p60"></a>**60** And they shall overcome all things.

<a name="section-76_p61"></a>**61** Wherefore, let no man glory in man, but rather let him glory in God, who shall subdue all enemies under his feet.

<a name="section-76_p62"></a>**62** These shall dwell in the presence of God and his Christ forever and ever.

<a name="section-76_p63"></a>**63** These are they whom he shall bring with him, when he shall come in the clouds of heaven to reign on the earth over his people.

<a name="section-76_p64"></a>**64** These are they who shall have part in the first resurrection.

<a name="section-76_p65"></a>**65** These are they who shall come forth in the resurrection of the just.

<a name="section-76_p66"></a>**66** These are they who are come unto Mount Zion, and unto the city of the living God, the heavenly place, the holiest of all.

<a name="section-76_p67"></a>**67** These are they who have come to an innumerable company of angels, to the general assembly and church of Enoch, and of the Firstborn.

<a name="section-76_p68"></a>**68** These are they whose names are written in heaven, where God and Christ are the judge of all.

<a name="section-76_p69"></a>**69** These are they who are just men made perfect through Jesus the mediator of the new covenant, who wrought out this perfect atonement through the shedding of his own blood.

<a name="section-76_p70"></a>**70** These are they whose bodies are celestial, whose glory is that of the sun, even the glory of God, the highest of all, whose glory the sun of the firmament is written of as being typical.

<a name="section-76_p71"></a>**71** And again, we saw the terrestrial world, and behold and lo, these are they who are of the terrestrial, whose glory differs from that of the church of the Firstborn who have received the fulness of the Father, even as that of the moon differs from the sun in the firmament.

<a name="section-76_p72"></a>**72** Behold, these are they who died without law;

<a name="section-76_p73"></a>**73** And also they who are the spirits of men kept in prison, whom the Son visited, and preached the gospel unto them, that they might be judged according to men in the flesh;

<a name="section-76_p74"></a>**74** Who received not the testimony of Jesus in the flesh, but afterwards received it.

<a name="section-76_p75"></a>**75** These are they who are honorable men of the earth, who were blinded by the craftiness of men.

<a name="section-76_p76"></a>**76** These are they who receive of his glory, but not of his fulness.

<a name="section-76_p77"></a>**77** These are they who receive of the presence of the Son, but not of the fulness of the Father.

<a name="section-76_p78"></a>**78** Wherefore, they are bodies terrestrial, and not bodies celestial, and differ in glory as the moon differs from the sun.

<a name="section-76_p79"></a>**79** These are they who are not valiant in the testimony of Jesus; wherefore, they obtain not the crown over the kingdom of our God.

<a name="section-76_p80"></a>**80** And now this is the end of the vision which we saw of the terrestrial, that the Lord commanded us to write while we were yet in the Spirit.

<a name="section-76_p81"></a>**81** And again, we saw the glory of the telestial, which glory is that of the lesser, even as the glory of the stars differs from that of the glory of the moon in the firmament.

<a name="section-76_p82"></a>**82** These are they who received not the gospel of Christ, neither the testimony of Jesus.

<a name="section-76_p83"></a>**83** These are they who deny not the Holy Spirit.

<a name="section-76_p84"></a>**84** These are they who are thrust down to hell.

<a name="section-76_p85"></a>**85** These are they who shall not be redeemed from the devil until the last resurrection, until the Lord, even Christ the Lamb, shall have finished his work.

<a name="section-76_p86"></a>**86** These are they who receive not of his fulness in the eternal world, but of the Holy Spirit through the ministration of the terrestrial;

<a name="section-76_p87"></a>**87** And the terrestrial through the ministration of the celestial.

<a name="section-76_p88"></a>**88** And also the telestial receive it of the administering of angels who are appointed to minister for them, or who are appointed to be ministering spirits for them; for they shall be heirs of salvation.

<a name="section-76_p89"></a>**89** And thus we saw, in the heavenly vision, the glory of the telestial, which surpasses all understanding;

<a name="section-76_p90"></a>**90** And no man knows it except him to whom God has revealed it.

<a name="section-76_p91"></a>**91** And thus we saw the glory of the terrestrial which excels in all things the glory of the telestial, even in glory, and in power, and in might, and in dominion.

<a name="section-76_p92"></a>**92** And thus we saw the glory of the celestial, which excels in all things—where God, even the Father, reigns upon his throne forever and ever;

<a name="section-76_p93"></a>**93** Before whose throne all things bow in humble reverence, and give him glory forever and ever.

<a name="section-76_p94"></a>**94** They who dwell in his presence are the church of the Firstborn; and they see as they are seen, and know as they are known, having received of his fulness and of his grace;

<a name="section-76_p95"></a>**95** And he makes them equal in power, and in might, and in dominion.

<a name="section-76_p96"></a>**96** And the glory of the celestial is one, even as the glory of the sun is one.

<a name="section-76_p97"></a>**97** And the glory of the terrestrial is one, even as the glory of the moon is one.

<a name="section-76_p98"></a>**98** And the glory of the telestial is one, even as the glory of the stars is one; for as one star differs from another star in glory, even so differs one from another in glory in the telestial world;

<a name="section-76_p99"></a>**99** For these are they who are of Paul, and of Apollos, and of Cephas.

<a name="section-76_p100"></a>**100** These are they who say they are some of one and some of another—some of Christ and some of John, and some of Moses, and some of Elias, and some of Esaias, and some of Isaiah, and some of Enoch;

<a name="section-76_p101"></a>**101** But received not the gospel, neither the testimony of Jesus, neither the prophets, neither the everlasting covenant.

<a name="section-76_p102"></a>**102** Last of all, these all are they who will not be gathered with the saints, to be caught up unto the church of the Firstborn, and received into the cloud.

<a name="section-76_p103"></a>**103** These are they who are liars, and sorcerers, and adulterers, and whoremongers, and whosoever loves and makes a lie.

<a name="section-76_p104"></a>**104** These are they who suffer the wrath of God on earth.

<a name="section-76_p105"></a>**105** These are they who suffer the vengeance of eternal fire.

<a name="section-76_p106"></a>**106** These are they who are cast down to hell and suffer the wrath of Almighty God, until the fulness of times, when Christ shall have subdued all enemies under his feet, and shall have perfected his work;

<a name="section-76_p107"></a>**107** When he shall deliver up the kingdom, and present it unto the Father, spotless, saying: I have overcome and have trodden the wine-press alone, even the wine-press of the fierceness of the wrath of Almighty God.

<a name="section-76_p108"></a>**108** Then shall he be crowned with the crown of his glory, to sit on the throne of his power to reign forever and ever.

<a name="section-76_p109"></a>**109** But behold, and lo, we saw the glory and the inhabitants of the telestial world, that they were as innumerable as the stars in the firmament of heaven, or as the sand upon the seashore;

<a name="section-76_p110"></a>**110** And heard the voice of the Lord saying: These all shall bow the knee, and every tongue shall confess to him who sits upon the throne forever and ever;

<a name="section-76_p111"></a>**111** For they shall be judged according to their works, and every man shall receive according to his own works, his own dominion, in the mansions which are prepared;

<a name="section-76_p112"></a>**112** And they shall be servants of the Most High; but where God and Christ dwell they cannot come, worlds without end.

<a name="section-76_p113"></a>**113** This is the end of the vision which we saw, which we were commanded to write while we were yet in the Spirit.

<a name="section-76_p114"></a>**114** But great and marvelous are the works of the Lord, and the mysteries of his kingdom which he showed unto us, which surpass all understanding in glory, and in might, and in dominion;

<a name="section-76_p115"></a>**115** Which he commanded us we should not write while we were yet in the Spirit, and are not lawful for man to utter;

<a name="section-76_p116"></a>**116** Neither is man capable to make them known, for they are only to be seen and understood by the power of the Holy Spirit, which God bestows on those who love him, and purify themselves before him;

<a name="section-76_p117"></a>**117** To whom he grants this privilege of seeing and knowing for themselves;

<a name="section-76_p118"></a>**118** That through the power and manifestation of the Spirit, while in the flesh, they may be able to bear his presence in the world of glory.

<a name="section-76_p119"></a>**119** And to God and the Lamb be glory, and honor, and dominion forever and ever. Amen.


---

## <a name="section-77"></a>Section 77

<a name="section-77_p1"></a>**1** Q. What is the sea of glass spoken of by John, 4th chapter, and 6th verse of the Revelation?  

A. It is the earth, in its sanctified, immortal, and eternal state.

<a name="section-77_p2"></a>**2** Q. What are we to understand by the four beasts, spoken of in the same verse?  

A. They are figurative expressions, used by the Revelator, John, in describing heaven, the paradise of God, the happiness of man, and of beasts, and of creeping things, and of the fowls of the air; that which is spiritual being in the likeness of that which is temporal; and that which is temporal in the likeness of that which is spiritual; the spirit of man in the likeness of his person, as also the spirit of the beast, and every other creature which God has created.

<a name="section-77_p3"></a>**3** Q. Are the four beasts limited to individual beasts, or do they represent classes or orders?  

A. They are limited to four individual beasts, which were shown to John, to represent the glory of the classes of beings in their destined order or sphere of creation, in the enjoyment of their eternal felicity.

<a name="section-77_p4"></a>**4** Q. What are we to understand by the eyes and wings, which the beasts had?  

A. Their eyes are a representation of light and knowledge, that is, they are full of knowledge; and their wings are a representation of power, to move, to act, etc.

<a name="section-77_p5"></a>**5** Q. What are we to understand by the four and twenty elders, spoken of by John?  

A. We are to understand that these elders whom John saw, were elders who had been faithful in the work of the ministry and were dead; who belonged to the seven churches, and were then in the paradise of God.

<a name="section-77_p6"></a>**6** Q. What are we to understand by the book which John saw, which was sealed on the back with seven seals?  

A. We are to understand that it contains the revealed will, mysteries, and the works of God; the hidden things of his economy concerning this earth during the seven thousand years of its continuance, or its temporal existence.

<a name="section-77_p7"></a>**7** Q. What are we to understand by the seven seals with which it was sealed?  

A. We are to understand that the first seal contains the things of the first thousand years, and the second also of the second thousand years, and so on until the seventh.

<a name="section-77_p8"></a>**8** Q. What are we to understand by the four angels, spoken of in the 7th chapter and 1st verse of Revelation?  

A. We are to understand that they are four angels sent forth from God, to whom is given power over the four parts of the earth, to save life and to destroy; these are they who have the everlasting gospel to commit to every nation, kindred, tongue, and people; having power to shut up the heavens, to seal up unto life, or to cast down to the regions of darkness.

<a name="section-77_p9"></a>**9** Q. What are we to understand by the angel ascending from the east, Revelation 7th chapter and 2nd verse?  

A. We are to understand that the angel ascending from the east is he to whom is given the seal of the living God over the twelve tribes of Israel; wherefore, he crieth unto the four angels having the everlasting gospel, saying: Hurt not the earth, neither the sea, nor the trees, till we have sealed the servants of our God in their foreheads. And, if you will receive it, this is Elias which was to come to gather together the tribes of Israel and restore all things.

<a name="section-77_p10"></a>**10** Q. What time are the things spoken of in this chapter to be accomplished?  

A. They are to be accomplished in the sixth thousand years, or the opening of the sixth seal.

<a name="section-77_p11"></a>**11** Q. What are we to understand by sealing the one hundred and forty-four thousand, out of all the tribes of Israel—twelve thousand out of every tribe?  

A. We are to understand that those who are sealed are high priests, ordained unto the holy order of God, to administer the everlasting gospel; for they are they who are ordained out of every nation, kindred, tongue, and people, by the angels to whom is given power over the nations of the earth, to bring as many as will come to the church of the Firstborn.

<a name="section-77_p12"></a>**12** Q. What are we to understand by the sounding of the trumpets, mentioned in the 8th chapter of Revelation?  

A. We are to understand that as God made the world in six days, and on the seventh day he finished his work, and sanctified it, and also formed man out of the dust of the earth, even so, in the beginning of the seventh thousand years will the Lord God sanctify the earth, and complete the salvation of man, and judge all things, and shall redeem all things, except that which he hath not put into his power, when he shall have sealed all things, unto the end of all things; and the sounding of the trumpets of the seven angels are the preparing and finishing of his work, in the beginning of the seventh thousand years—the preparing of the way before the time of his coming.

<a name="section-77_p13"></a>**13** Q. When are the things to be accomplished, which are written in the 9th chapter of Revelation?  

A. They are to be accomplished after the opening of the seventh seal, before the coming of Christ.

<a name="section-77_p14"></a>**14** Q. What are we to understand by the little book which was eaten by John, as mentioned in the 10th chapter of Revelation?  

A. We are to understand that it was a mission, and an ordinance, for him to gather the tribes of Israel; behold, this is Elias, who, as it is written, must come and restore all things.

<a name="section-77_p15"></a>**15** Q. What is to be understood by the two witnesses, in the eleventh chapter of Revelation?  

A. They are two prophets that are to be raised up to the Jewish nation in the last days, at the time of the restoration, and to prophesy to the Jews after they are gathered and have built the city of Jerusalem in the land of their fathers.


---

## <a name="section-78"></a>Section 78

<a name="section-78_p1"></a>**1** The Lord spake unto Joseph Smith, Jun., saying: Hearken unto me, saith the Lord your God, who are ordained unto the high priesthood of my church, who have assembled yourselves together;

<a name="section-78_p2"></a>**2** And listen to the counsel of him who has ordained you from on high, who shall speak in your ears the words of wisdom, that salvation may be unto you in that thing which you have presented before me, saith the Lord God.

<a name="section-78_p3"></a>**3** For verily I say unto you, the time has come, and is now at hand; and behold, and lo, it must needs be that there be an organization of my people, in regulating and establishing the affairs of the storehouse for the poor of my people, both in this place and in the land of Zion—

<a name="section-78_p4"></a>**4** For a permanent and everlasting establishment and order unto my church, to advance the cause, which ye have espoused, to the salvation of man, and to the glory of your Father who is in heaven;

<a name="section-78_p5"></a>**5** That you may be equal in the bonds of heavenly things, yea, and earthly things also, for the obtaining of heavenly things.

<a name="section-78_p6"></a>**6** For if ye are not equal in earthly things ye cannot be equal in obtaining heavenly things;

<a name="section-78_p7"></a>**7** For if you will that I give unto you a place in the celestial world, you must prepare yourselves by doing the things which I have commanded you and required of you.

<a name="section-78_p8"></a>**8** And now, verily thus saith the Lord, it is expedient that all things be done unto my glory, by you who are joined together in this order;

<a name="section-78_p9"></a>**9** Or, in other words, let my servant Newel K. Whitney and my servant Joseph Smith, Jun., and my servant Sidney Rigdon sit in council with the saints which are in Zion;

<a name="section-78_p10"></a>**10** Otherwise Satan seeketh to turn their hearts away from the truth, that they become blinded and understand not the things which are prepared for them.

<a name="section-78_p11"></a>**11** Wherefore, a commandment I give unto you, to prepare and organize yourselves by a bond or everlasting covenant that cannot be broken.

<a name="section-78_p12"></a>**12** And he who breaketh it shall lose his office and standing in the church, and shall be delivered over to the buffetings of Satan until the day of redemption.

<a name="section-78_p13"></a>**13** Behold, this is the preparation wherewith I prepare you, and the foundation, and the ensample which I give unto you, whereby you may accomplish the commandments which are given you;

<a name="section-78_p14"></a>**14** That through my providence, notwithstanding the tribulation which shall descend upon you, that the church may stand independent above all other creatures beneath the celestial world;

<a name="section-78_p15"></a>**15** That you may come up unto the crown prepared for you, and be made rulers over many kingdoms, saith the Lord God, the Holy One of Zion, who hath established the foundations of Adam-ondi-Ahman;

<a name="section-78_p16"></a>**16** Who hath appointed Michael your prince, and established his feet, and set him upon high, and given unto him the keys of salvation under the counsel and direction of the Holy One, who is without beginning of days or end of life.

<a name="section-78_p17"></a>**17** Verily, verily, I say unto you, ye are little children, and ye have not as yet understood how great blessings the Father hath in his own hands and prepared for you;

<a name="section-78_p18"></a>**18** And ye cannot bear all things now; nevertheless, be of good cheer, for I will lead you along. The kingdom is yours and the blessings thereof are yours, and the riches of eternity are yours.

<a name="section-78_p19"></a>**19** And he who receiveth all things with thankfulness shall be made glorious; and the things of this earth shall be added unto him, even an hundred fold, yea, more.

<a name="section-78_p20"></a>**20** Wherefore, do the things which I have commanded you, saith your Redeemer, even the Son Ahman, who prepareth all things before he taketh you;

<a name="section-78_p21"></a>**21** For ye are the church of the Firstborn, and he will take you up in a cloud, and appoint every man his portion.

<a name="section-78_p22"></a>**22** And he that is a faithful and wise steward shall inherit all things. Amen.


---

## <a name="section-79"></a>Section 79

<a name="section-79_p1"></a>**1** Verily I say unto you, that it is my will that my servant Jared Carter should go again into the eastern countries, from place to place, and from city to city, in the power of the ordination wherewith he has been ordained, proclaiming glad tidings of great joy, even the everlasting gospel.

<a name="section-79_p2"></a>**2** And I will send upon him the Comforter, which shall teach him the truth and the way whither he shall go;

<a name="section-79_p3"></a>**3** And inasmuch as he is faithful, I will crown him again with sheaves.

<a name="section-79_p4"></a>**4** Wherefore, let your heart be glad, my servant Jared Carter, and fear not, saith your Lord, even Jesus Christ. Amen.


---

## <a name="section-80"></a>Section 80

<a name="section-80_p1"></a>**1** Verily, thus saith the Lord unto you my servant Stephen Burnett: Go ye, go ye into the world and preach the gospel to every creature that cometh under the sound of your voice.

<a name="section-80_p2"></a>**2** And inasmuch as you desire a companion, I will give unto you my servant Eden Smith.

<a name="section-80_p3"></a>**3** Wherefore, go ye and preach my gospel, whether to the north or to the south, to the east or to the west, it mattereth not, for ye cannot go amiss.

<a name="section-80_p4"></a>**4** Therefore, declare the things which ye have heard, and verily believe, and know to be true.

<a name="section-80_p5"></a>**5** Behold, this is the will of him who hath called you, your Redeemer, even Jesus Christ. Amen.


---

## <a name="section-81"></a>Section 81

<a name="section-81_p1"></a>**1** Verily, verily, I say unto you my servant Frederick G. Williams: Listen to the voice of him who speaketh, to the word of the Lord your God, and hearken to the calling wherewith you are called, even to be a high priest in my church, and a counselor unto my servant Joseph Smith, Jun.;

<a name="section-81_p2"></a>**2** Unto whom I have given the keys of the kingdom, which belong always unto the Presidency of the High Priesthood:

<a name="section-81_p3"></a>**3** Therefore, verily I acknowledge him and will bless him, and also thee, inasmuch as thou art faithful in counsel, in the office which I have appointed unto you, in prayer always, vocally and in thy heart, in public and in private, also in thy ministry in proclaiming the gospel in the land of the living, and among thy brethren.

<a name="section-81_p4"></a>**4** And in doing these things thou wilt do the greatest good unto thy fellow beings, and wilt promote the glory of him who is your Lord.

<a name="section-81_p5"></a>**5** Wherefore, be faithful; stand in the office which I have appointed unto you; succor the weak, lift up the hands which hang down, and strengthen the feeble knees.

<a name="section-81_p6"></a>**6** And if thou art faithful unto the end thou shalt have a crown of immortality, and eternal life in the mansions which I have prepared in the house of my Father.

<a name="section-81_p7"></a>**7** Behold, and lo, these are the words of Alpha and Omega, even Jesus Christ. Amen.


---

## <a name="section-82"></a>Section 82

<a name="section-82_p1"></a>**1** Verily, verily, I say unto you, my servants, that inasmuch as you have forgiven one another your trespasses, even so I, the Lord, forgive you.

<a name="section-82_p2"></a>**2** Nevertheless, there are those among you who have sinned exceedingly; yea, even all of you have sinned; but verily I say unto you, beware from henceforth, and refrain from sin, lest sore judgments fall upon your heads.

<a name="section-82_p3"></a>**3** For of him unto whom much is given much is required; and he who sins against the greater light shall receive the greater condemnation.

<a name="section-82_p4"></a>**4** Ye call upon my name for revelations, and I give them unto you; and inasmuch as ye keep not my sayings, which I give unto you, ye become transgressors; and justice and judgment are the penalty which is affixed unto my law.

<a name="section-82_p5"></a>**5** Therefore, what I say unto one I say unto all: Watch, for the adversary spreadeth his dominions, and darkness reigneth;

<a name="section-82_p6"></a>**6** And the anger of God kindleth against the inhabitants of the earth; and none doeth good, for all have gone out of the way.

<a name="section-82_p7"></a>**7** And now, verily I say unto you, I, the Lord, will not lay any sin to your charge; go your ways and sin no more; but unto that soul who sinneth shall the former sins return, saith the Lord your God.

<a name="section-82_p8"></a>**8** And again, I say unto you, I give unto you a new commandment, that you may understand my will concerning you;

<a name="section-82_p9"></a>**9** Or, in other words, I give unto you directions how you may act before me, that it may turn to you for your salvation.

<a name="section-82_p10"></a>**10** I, the Lord, am bound when ye do what I say; but when ye do not what I say, ye have no promise.

<a name="section-82_p11"></a>**11** Therefore, verily I say unto you, that it is expedient for my servants Edward Partridge and Newel K. Whitney, A. Sidney Gilbert and Sidney Rigdon, and my servant Joseph Smith, and John Whitmer and Oliver Cowdery, and W. W. Phelps and Martin Harris to be bound together by a bond and covenant that cannot be broken by transgression, except judgment shall immediately follow, in your several stewardships—

<a name="section-82_p12"></a>**12** To manage the affairs of the poor, and all things pertaining to the bishopric both in the land of Zion and in the land of Kirtland;

<a name="section-82_p13"></a>**13** For I have consecrated the land of Kirtland in mine own due time for the benefit of the saints of the Most High, and for a stake to Zion.

<a name="section-82_p14"></a>**14** For Zion must increase in beauty, and in holiness; her borders must be enlarged; her stakes must be strengthened; yea, verily I say unto you, Zion must arise and put on her beautiful garments.

<a name="section-82_p15"></a>**15** Therefore, I give unto you this commandment, that ye bind yourselves by this covenant, and it shall be done according to the laws of the Lord.

<a name="section-82_p16"></a>**16** Behold, here is wisdom also in me for your good.

<a name="section-82_p17"></a>**17** And you are to be equal, or in other words, you are to have equal claims on the properties, for the benefit of managing the concerns of your stewardships, every man according to his wants and his needs, inasmuch as his wants are just—

<a name="section-82_p18"></a>**18** And all this for the benefit of the church of the living God, that every man may improve upon his talent, that every man may gain other talents, yea, even an hundred fold, to be cast into the Lord’s storehouse, to become the common property of the whole church—

<a name="section-82_p19"></a>**19** Every man seeking the interest of his neighbor, and doing all things with an eye single to the glory of God.

<a name="section-82_p20"></a>**20** This order I have appointed to be an everlasting order unto you, and unto your successors, inasmuch as you sin not.

<a name="section-82_p21"></a>**21** And the soul that sins against this covenant, and hardeneth his heart against it, shall be dealt with according to the laws of my church, and shall be delivered over to the buffetings of Satan until the day of redemption.

<a name="section-82_p22"></a>**22** And now, verily I say unto you, and this is wisdom, make unto yourselves friends with the mammon of unrighteousness, and they will not destroy you.

<a name="section-82_p23"></a>**23** Leave judgment alone with me, for it is mine and I will repay. Peace be with you; my blessings continue with you.

<a name="section-82_p24"></a>**24** For even yet the kingdom is yours, and shall be forever, if you fall not from your steadfastness. Even so. Amen.


---

## <a name="section-83"></a>Section 83

<a name="section-83_p1"></a>**1** Verily, thus saith the Lord, in addition to the laws of the church concerning women and children, those who belong to the church, who have lost their husbands or fathers:

<a name="section-83_p2"></a>**2** Women have claim on their husbands for their maintenance, until their husbands are taken; and if they are not found transgressors they shall have fellowship in the church.

<a name="section-83_p3"></a>**3** And if they are not faithful they shall not have fellowship in the church; yet they may remain upon their inheritances according to the laws of the land.

<a name="section-83_p4"></a>**4** All children have claim upon their parents for their maintenance until they are of age.

<a name="section-83_p5"></a>**5** And after that, they have claim upon the church, or in other words upon the Lord’s storehouse, if their parents have not wherewith to give them inheritances.

<a name="section-83_p6"></a>**6** And the storehouse shall be kept by the consecrations of the church; and widows and orphans shall be provided for, as also the poor. Amen.


---

## <a name="section-84"></a>Section 84

<a name="section-84_p1"></a>**1** A revelation of Jesus Christ unto his servant Joseph Smith, Jun., and six elders, as they united their hearts and lifted their voices on high.

<a name="section-84_p2"></a>**2** Yea, the word of the Lord concerning his church, established in the last days for the restoration of his people, as he has spoken by the mouth of his prophets, and for the gathering of his saints to stand upon Mount Zion, which shall be the city of New Jerusalem.

<a name="section-84_p3"></a>**3** Which city shall be built, beginning at the temple lot, which is appointed by the finger of the Lord, in the western boundaries of the State of Missouri, and dedicated by the hand of Joseph Smith, Jun., and others with whom the Lord was well pleased.

<a name="section-84_p4"></a>**4** Verily this is the word of the Lord, that the city New Jerusalem shall be built by the gathering of the saints, beginning at this place, even the place of the temple, which temple shall be reared in this generation.

<a name="section-84_p5"></a>**5** For verily this generation shall not all pass away until an house shall be built unto the Lord, and a cloud shall rest upon it, which cloud shall be even the glory of the Lord, which shall fill the house.

<a name="section-84_p6"></a>**6** And the sons of Moses, according to the Holy Priesthood which he received under the hand of his father-in-law, Jethro;

<a name="section-84_p7"></a>**7** And Jethro received it under the hand of Caleb;

<a name="section-84_p8"></a>**8** And Caleb received it under the hand of Elihu;

<a name="section-84_p9"></a>**9** And Elihu under the hand of Jeremy;

<a name="section-84_p10"></a>**10** And Jeremy under the hand of Gad;

<a name="section-84_p11"></a>**11** And Gad under the hand of Esaias;

<a name="section-84_p12"></a>**12** And Esaias received it under the hand of God.

<a name="section-84_p13"></a>**13** Esaias also lived in the days of Abraham, and was blessed of him—

<a name="section-84_p14"></a>**14** Which Abraham received the priesthood from Melchizedek, who received it through the lineage of his fathers, even till Noah;

<a name="section-84_p15"></a>**15** And from Noah till Enoch, through the lineage of their fathers;

<a name="section-84_p16"></a>**16** And from Enoch to Abel, who was slain by the conspiracy of his brother, who received the priesthood by the commandments of God, by the hand of his father Adam, who was the first man—

<a name="section-84_p17"></a>**17** Which priesthood continueth in the church of God in all generations, and is without beginning of days or end of years.

<a name="section-84_p18"></a>**18** And the Lord confirmed a priesthood also upon Aaron and his seed, throughout all their generations, which priesthood also continueth and abideth forever with the priesthood which is after the holiest order of God.

<a name="section-84_p19"></a>**19** And this greater priesthood administereth the gospel and holdeth the key of the mysteries of the kingdom, even the key of the knowledge of God.

<a name="section-84_p20"></a>**20** Therefore, in the ordinances thereof, the power of godliness is manifest.

<a name="section-84_p21"></a>**21** And without the ordinances thereof, and the authority of the priesthood, the power of godliness is not manifest unto men in the flesh;

<a name="section-84_p22"></a>**22** For without this no man can see the face of God, even the Father, and live.

<a name="section-84_p23"></a>**23** Now this Moses plainly taught to the children of Israel in the wilderness, and sought diligently to sanctify his people that they might behold the face of God;

<a name="section-84_p24"></a>**24** But they hardened their hearts and could not endure his presence; therefore, the Lord in his wrath, for his anger was kindled against them, swore that they should not enter into his rest while in the wilderness, which rest is the fulness of his glory.

<a name="section-84_p25"></a>**25** Therefore, he took Moses out of their midst, and the Holy Priesthood also;

<a name="section-84_p26"></a>**26** And the lesser priesthood continued, which priesthood holdeth the key of the ministering of angels and the preparatory gospel;

<a name="section-84_p27"></a>**27** Which gospel is the gospel of repentance and of baptism, and the remission of sins, and the law of carnal commandments, which the Lord in his wrath caused to continue with the house of Aaron among the children of Israel until John, whom God raised up, being filled with the Holy Ghost from his mother’s womb.

<a name="section-84_p28"></a>**28** For he was baptized while he was yet in his childhood, and was ordained by the angel of God at the time he was eight days old unto this power, to overthrow the kingdom of the Jews, and to make straight the way of the Lord before the face of his people, to prepare them for the coming of the Lord, in whose hand is given all power.

<a name="section-84_p29"></a>**29** And again, the offices of elder and bishop are necessary appendages belonging unto the high priesthood.

<a name="section-84_p30"></a>**30** And again, the offices of teacher and deacon are necessary appendages belonging to the lesser priesthood, which priesthood was confirmed upon Aaron and his sons.

<a name="section-84_p31"></a>**31** Therefore, as I said concerning the sons of Moses—for the sons of Moses and also the sons of Aaron shall offer an acceptable offering and sacrifice in the house of the Lord, which house shall be built unto the Lord in this generation, upon the consecrated spot as I have appointed—

<a name="section-84_p32"></a>**32** And the sons of Moses and of Aaron shall be filled with the glory of the Lord, upon Mount Zion in the Lord’s house, whose sons are ye; and also many whom I have called and sent forth to build up my church.

<a name="section-84_p33"></a>**33** For whoso is faithful unto the obtaining these two priesthoods of which I have spoken, and the magnifying their calling, are sanctified by the Spirit unto the renewing of their bodies.

<a name="section-84_p34"></a>**34** They become the sons of Moses and of Aaron and the seed of Abraham, and the church and kingdom, and the elect of God.

<a name="section-84_p35"></a>**35** And also all they who receive this priesthood receive me, saith the Lord;

<a name="section-84_p36"></a>**36** For he that receiveth my servants receiveth me;

<a name="section-84_p37"></a>**37** And he that receiveth me receiveth my Father;

<a name="section-84_p38"></a>**38** And he that receiveth my Father receiveth my Father’s kingdom; therefore all that my Father hath shall be given unto him.

<a name="section-84_p39"></a>**39** And this is according to the oath and covenant which belongeth to the priesthood.

<a name="section-84_p40"></a>**40** Therefore, all those who receive the priesthood, receive this oath and covenant of my Father, which he cannot break, neither can it be moved.

<a name="section-84_p41"></a>**41** But whoso breaketh this covenant after he hath received it, and altogether turneth therefrom, shall not have forgiveness of sins in this world nor in the world to come.

<a name="section-84_p42"></a>**42** And wo unto all those who come not unto this priesthood which ye have received, which I now confirm upon you who are present this day, by mine own voice out of the heavens; and even I have given the heavenly hosts and mine angels charge concerning you.

<a name="section-84_p43"></a>**43** And I now give unto you a commandment to beware concerning yourselves, to give diligent heed to the words of eternal life.

<a name="section-84_p44"></a>**44** For you shall live by every word that proceedeth forth from the mouth of God.

<a name="section-84_p45"></a>**45** For the word of the Lord is truth, and whatsoever is truth is light, and whatsoever is light is Spirit, even the Spirit of Jesus Christ.

<a name="section-84_p46"></a>**46** And the Spirit giveth light to every man that cometh into the world; and the Spirit enlighteneth every man through the world, that hearkeneth to the voice of the Spirit.

<a name="section-84_p47"></a>**47** And every one that hearkeneth to the voice of the Spirit cometh unto God, even the Father.

<a name="section-84_p48"></a>**48** And the Father teacheth him of the covenant which he has renewed and confirmed upon you, which is confirmed upon you for your sakes, and not for your sakes only, but for the sake of the whole world.

<a name="section-84_p49"></a>**49** And the whole world lieth in sin, and groaneth under darkness and under the bondage of sin.

<a name="section-84_p50"></a>**50** And by this you may know they are under the bondage of sin, because they come not unto me.

<a name="section-84_p51"></a>**51** For whoso cometh not unto me is under the bondage of sin.

<a name="section-84_p52"></a>**52** And whoso receiveth not my voice is not acquainted with my voice, and is not of me.

<a name="section-84_p53"></a>**53** And by this you may know the righteous from the wicked, and that the whole world groaneth under sin and darkness even now.

<a name="section-84_p54"></a>**54** And your minds in times past have been darkened because of unbelief, and because you have treated lightly the things you have received—

<a name="section-84_p55"></a>**55** Which vanity and unbelief have brought the whole church under condemnation.

<a name="section-84_p56"></a>**56** And this condemnation resteth upon the children of Zion, even all.

<a name="section-84_p57"></a>**57** And they shall remain under this condemnation until they repent and remember the new covenant, even the Book of Mormon and the former commandments which I have given them, not only to say, but to do according to that which I have written—

<a name="section-84_p58"></a>**58** That they may bring forth fruit meet for their Father’s kingdom; otherwise there remaineth a scourge and judgment to be poured out upon the children of Zion.

<a name="section-84_p59"></a>**59** For shall the children of the kingdom pollute my holy land? Verily, I say unto you, Nay.

<a name="section-84_p60"></a>**60** Verily, verily, I say unto you who now hear my words, which are my voice, blessed are ye inasmuch as you receive these things;

<a name="section-84_p61"></a>**61** For I will forgive you of your sins with this commandment—that you remain steadfast in your minds in solemnity and the spirit of prayer, in bearing testimony to all the world of those things which are communicated unto you.

<a name="section-84_p62"></a>**62** Therefore, go ye into all the world; and unto whatsoever place ye cannot go ye shall send, that the testimony may go from you into all the world unto every creature.

<a name="section-84_p63"></a>**63** And as I said unto mine apostles, even so I say unto you, for you are mine apostles, even God’s high priests; ye are they whom my Father hath given me; ye are my friends;

<a name="section-84_p64"></a>**64** Therefore, as I said unto mine apostles I say unto you again, that every soul who believeth on your words, and is baptized by water for the remission of sins, shall receive the Holy Ghost.

<a name="section-84_p65"></a>**65** And these signs shall follow them that believe—

<a name="section-84_p66"></a>**66** In my name they shall do many wonderful works;

<a name="section-84_p67"></a>**67** In my name they shall cast out devils;

<a name="section-84_p68"></a>**68** In my name they shall heal the sick;

<a name="section-84_p69"></a>**69** In my name they shall open the eyes of the blind, and unstop the ears of the deaf;

<a name="section-84_p70"></a>**70** And the tongue of the dumb shall speak;

<a name="section-84_p71"></a>**71** And if any man shall administer poison unto them it shall not hurt them;

<a name="section-84_p72"></a>**72** And the poison of a serpent shall not have power to harm them.

<a name="section-84_p73"></a>**73** But a commandment I give unto them, that they shall not boast themselves of these things, neither speak them before the world; for these things are given unto you for your profit and for salvation.

<a name="section-84_p74"></a>**74** Verily, verily, I say unto you, they who believe not on your words, and are not baptized in water in my name, for the remission of their sins, that they may receive the Holy Ghost, shall be damned, and shall not come into my Father’s kingdom where my Father and I am.

<a name="section-84_p75"></a>**75** And this revelation unto you, and commandment, is in force from this very hour upon all the world, and the gospel is unto all who have not received it.

<a name="section-84_p76"></a>**76** But, verily I say unto all those to whom the kingdom has been given—from you it must be preached unto them, that they shall repent of their former evil works; for they are to be upbraided for their evil hearts of unbelief, and your brethren in Zion for their rebellion against you at the time I sent you.

<a name="section-84_p77"></a>**77** And again I say unto you, my friends, for from henceforth I shall call you friends, it is expedient that I give unto you this commandment, that ye become even as my friends in days when I was with them, traveling to preach the gospel in my power;

<a name="section-84_p78"></a>**78** For I suffered them not to have purse or scrip, neither two coats.

<a name="section-84_p79"></a>**79** Behold, I send you out to prove the world, and the laborer is worthy of his hire.

<a name="section-84_p80"></a>**80** And any man that shall go and preach this gospel of the kingdom, and fail not to continue faithful in all things, shall not be weary in mind, neither darkened, neither in body, limb, nor joint; and a hair of his head shall not fall to the ground unnoticed. And they shall not go hungry, neither athirst.

<a name="section-84_p81"></a>**81** Therefore, take ye no thought for the morrow, for what ye shall eat, or what ye shall drink, or wherewithal ye shall be clothed.

<a name="section-84_p82"></a>**82** For, consider the lilies of the field, how they grow, they toil not, neither do they spin; and the kingdoms of the world, in all their glory, are not arrayed like one of these.

<a name="section-84_p83"></a>**83** For your Father, who is in heaven, knoweth that you have need of all these things.

<a name="section-84_p84"></a>**84** Therefore, let the morrow take thought for the things of itself.

<a name="section-84_p85"></a>**85** Neither take ye thought beforehand what ye shall say; but treasure up in your minds continually the words of life, and it shall be given you in the very hour that portion that shall be meted unto every man.

<a name="section-84_p86"></a>**86** Therefore, let no man among you, for this commandment is unto all the faithful who are called of God in the church unto the ministry, from this hour take purse or scrip, that goeth forth to proclaim this gospel of the kingdom.

<a name="section-84_p87"></a>**87** Behold, I send you out to reprove the world of all their unrighteous deeds, and to teach them of a judgment which is to come.

<a name="section-84_p88"></a>**88** And whoso receiveth you, there I will be also, for I will go before your face. I will be on your right hand and on your left, and my Spirit shall be in your hearts, and mine angels round about you, to bear you up.

<a name="section-84_p89"></a>**89** Whoso receiveth you receiveth me; and the same will feed you, and clothe you, and give you money.

<a name="section-84_p90"></a>**90** And he who feeds you, or clothes you, or gives you money, shall in nowise lose his reward.

<a name="section-84_p91"></a>**91** And he that doeth not these things is not my disciple; by this you may know my disciples.

<a name="section-84_p92"></a>**92** He that receiveth you not, go away from him alone by yourselves, and cleanse your feet even with water, pure water, whether in heat or in cold, and bear testimony of it unto your Father which is in heaven, and return not again unto that man.

<a name="section-84_p93"></a>**93** And in whatsoever village or city ye enter, do likewise.

<a name="section-84_p94"></a>**94** Nevertheless, search diligently and spare not; and wo unto that house, or that village or city that rejecteth you, or your words, or your testimony concerning me.

<a name="section-84_p95"></a>**95** Wo, I say again, unto that house, or that village or city that rejecteth you, or your words, or your testimony of me;

<a name="section-84_p96"></a>**96** For I, the Almighty, have laid my hands upon the nations, to scourge them for their wickedness.

<a name="section-84_p97"></a>**97** And plagues shall go forth, and they shall not be taken from the earth until I have completed my work, which shall be cut short in righteousness—

<a name="section-84_p98"></a>**98** Until all shall know me, who remain, even from the least unto the greatest, and shall be filled with the knowledge of the Lord, and shall see eye to eye, and shall lift up their voice, and with the voice together sing this new song, saying:

<a name="section-84_p99"></a>**99** The Lord hath brought again Zion;  

The Lord hath redeemed his people, Israel,  

According to the election of grace,  

Which was brought to pass by the faith  

And covenant of their fathers.  



<a name="section-84_p100"></a>**100** The Lord hath redeemed his people;  

And Satan is bound and time is no longer.  

The Lord hath gathered all things in one.  

The Lord hath brought down Zion from above.  

The Lord hath brought up Zion from beneath.  



<a name="section-84_p101"></a>**101** The earth hath travailed and brought forth her strength;  

And truth is established in her bowels;  

And the heavens have smiled upon her;  

And she is clothed with the glory of her God;  

For he stands in the midst of his people.  



<a name="section-84_p102"></a>**102** Glory, and honor, and power, and might,  

Be ascribed to our God; for he is full of mercy,  

Justice, grace and truth, and peace,  

Forever and ever, Amen.  



<a name="section-84_p103"></a>**103** And again, verily, verily, I say unto you, it is expedient that every man who goes forth to proclaim mine everlasting gospel, that inasmuch as they have families, and receive money by gift, that they should send it unto them or make use of it for their benefit, as the Lord shall direct them, for thus it seemeth me good.

<a name="section-84_p104"></a>**104** And let all those who have not families, who receive money, send it up unto the bishop in Zion, or unto the bishop in Ohio, that it may be consecrated for the bringing forth of the revelations and the printing thereof, and for establishing Zion.

<a name="section-84_p105"></a>**105** And if any man shall give unto any of you a coat, or a suit, take the old and cast it unto the poor, and go on your way rejoicing.

<a name="section-84_p106"></a>**106** And if any man among you be strong in the Spirit, let him take with him him that is weak, that he may be edified in all meekness, that he may become strong also.

<a name="section-84_p107"></a>**107** Therefore, take with you those who are ordained unto the lesser priesthood, and send them before you to make appointments, and to prepare the way, and to fill appointments that you yourselves are not able to fill.

<a name="section-84_p108"></a>**108** Behold, this is the way that mine apostles, in ancient days, built up my church unto me.

<a name="section-84_p109"></a>**109** Therefore, let every man stand in his own office, and labor in his own calling; and let not the head say unto the feet it hath no need of the feet; for without the feet how shall the body be able to stand?

<a name="section-84_p110"></a>**110** Also the body hath need of every member, that all may be edified together, that the system may be kept perfect.

<a name="section-84_p111"></a>**111** And behold, the high priests should travel, and also the elders, and also the lesser priests; but the deacons and teachers should be appointed to watch over the church, to be standing ministers unto the church.

<a name="section-84_p112"></a>**112** And the bishop, Newel K. Whitney, also should travel round about and among all the churches, searching after the poor to administer to their wants by humbling the rich and the proud.

<a name="section-84_p113"></a>**113** He should also employ an agent to take charge and to do his secular business as he shall direct.

<a name="section-84_p114"></a>**114** Nevertheless, let the bishop go unto the city of New York, also to the city of Albany, and also to the city of Boston, and warn the people of those cities with the sound of the gospel, with a loud voice, of the desolation and utter abolishment which await them if they do reject these things.

<a name="section-84_p115"></a>**115** For if they do reject these things the hour of their judgment is nigh, and their house shall be left unto them desolate.

<a name="section-84_p116"></a>**116** Let him trust in me and he shall not be confounded; and a hair of his head shall not fall to the ground unnoticed.

<a name="section-84_p117"></a>**117** And verily I say unto you, the rest of my servants, go ye forth as your circumstances shall permit, in your several callings, unto the great and notable cities and villages, reproving the world in righteousness of all their unrighteous and ungodly deeds, setting forth clearly and understandingly the desolation of abomination in the last days.

<a name="section-84_p118"></a>**118** For, with you saith the Lord Almighty, I will rend their kingdoms; I will not only shake the earth, but the starry heavens shall tremble.

<a name="section-84_p119"></a>**119** For I, the Lord, have put forth my hand to exert the powers of heaven; ye cannot see it now, yet a little while and ye shall see it, and know that I am, and that I will come and reign with my people.

<a name="section-84_p120"></a>**120** I am Alpha and Omega, the beginning and the end. Amen.


---

## <a name="section-85"></a>Section 85

<a name="section-85_p1"></a>**1** It is the duty of the Lord’s clerk, whom he has appointed, to keep a history, and a general church record of all things that transpire in Zion, and of all those who consecrate properties, and receive inheritances legally from the bishop;

<a name="section-85_p2"></a>**2** And also their manner of life, their faith, and works; and also of the apostates who apostatize after receiving their inheritances.

<a name="section-85_p3"></a>**3** It is contrary to the will and commandment of God that those who receive not their inheritance by consecration, agreeable to his law, which he has given, that he may tithe his people, to prepare them against the day of vengeance and burning, should have their names enrolled with the people of God.

<a name="section-85_p4"></a>**4** Neither is their genealogy to be kept, or to be had where it may be found on any of the records or history of the church.

<a name="section-85_p5"></a>**5** Their names shall not be found, neither the names of the fathers, nor the names of the children written in the book of the law of God, saith the Lord of Hosts.

<a name="section-85_p6"></a>**6** Yea, thus saith the still small voice, which whispereth through and pierceth all things, and often times it maketh my bones to quake while it maketh manifest, saying:

<a name="section-85_p7"></a>**7** And it shall come to pass that I, the Lord God, will send one mighty and strong, holding the scepter of power in his hand, clothed with light for a covering, whose mouth shall utter words, eternal words; while his bowels shall be a fountain of truth, to set in order the house of God, and to arrange by lot the inheritances of the saints whose names are found, and the names of their fathers, and of their children, enrolled in the book of the law of God;

<a name="section-85_p8"></a>**8** While that man, who was called of God and appointed, that putteth forth his hand to steady the ark of God, shall fall by the shaft of death, like as a tree that is smitten by the vivid shaft of lightning.

<a name="section-85_p9"></a>**9** And all they who are not found written in the book of remembrance shall find none inheritance in that day, but they shall be cut asunder, and their portion shall be appointed them among unbelievers, where are wailing and gnashing of teeth.

<a name="section-85_p10"></a>**10** These things I say not of myself; therefore, as the Lord speaketh, he will also fulfil.

<a name="section-85_p11"></a>**11** And they who are of the High Priesthood, whose names are not found written in the book of the law, or that are found to have apostatized, or to have been cut off from the church, as well as the lesser priesthood, or the members, in that day shall not find an inheritance among the saints of the Most High;

<a name="section-85_p12"></a>**12** Therefore, it shall be done unto them as unto the children of the priest, as will be found recorded in the second chapter and sixty-first and second verses of Ezra.


---

## <a name="section-86"></a>Section 86

<a name="section-86_p1"></a>**1** Verily, thus saith the Lord unto you my servants, concerning the parable of the wheat and of the tares:

<a name="section-86_p2"></a>**2** Behold, verily I say, the field was the world, and the apostles were the sowers of the seed;

<a name="section-86_p3"></a>**3** And after they have fallen asleep the great persecutor of the church, the apostate, the whore, even Babylon, that maketh all nations to drink of her cup, in whose hearts the enemy, even Satan, sitteth to reign—behold he soweth the tares; wherefore, the tares choke the wheat and drive the church into the wilderness.

<a name="section-86_p4"></a>**4** But behold, in the last days, even now while the Lord is beginning to bring forth the word, and the blade is springing up and is yet tender—

<a name="section-86_p5"></a>**5** Behold, verily I say unto you, the angels are crying unto the Lord day and night, who are ready and waiting to be sent forth to reap down the fields;

<a name="section-86_p6"></a>**6** But the Lord saith unto them, pluck not up the tares while the blade is yet tender (for verily your faith is weak), lest you destroy the wheat also.

<a name="section-86_p7"></a>**7** Therefore, let the wheat and the tares grow together until the harvest is fully ripe; then ye shall first gather out the wheat from among the tares, and after the gathering of the wheat, behold and lo, the tares are bound in bundles, and the field remaineth to be burned.

<a name="section-86_p8"></a>**8** Therefore, thus saith the Lord unto you, with whom the priesthood hath continued through the lineage of your fathers—

<a name="section-86_p9"></a>**9** For ye are lawful heirs, according to the flesh, and have been hid from the world with Christ in God—

<a name="section-86_p10"></a>**10** Therefore your life and the priesthood have remained, and must needs remain through you and your lineage until the restoration of all things spoken by the mouths of all the holy prophets since the world began.

<a name="section-86_p11"></a>**11** Therefore, blessed are ye if ye continue in my goodness, a light unto the Gentiles, and through this priesthood, a savior unto my people Israel. The Lord hath said it. Amen.


---

## <a name="section-87"></a>Section 87

<a name="section-87_p1"></a>**1** Verily, thus saith the Lord concerning the wars that will shortly come to pass, beginning at the rebellion of South Carolina, which will eventually terminate in the death and misery of many souls;

<a name="section-87_p2"></a>**2** And the time will come that war will be poured out upon all nations, beginning at this place.

<a name="section-87_p3"></a>**3** For behold, the Southern States shall be divided against the Northern States, and the Southern States will call on other nations, even the nation of Great Britain, as it is called, and they shall also call upon other nations, in order to defend themselves against other nations; and then war shall be poured out upon all nations.

<a name="section-87_p4"></a>**4** And it shall come to pass, after many days, slaves shall rise up against their masters, who shall be marshaled and disciplined for war.

<a name="section-87_p5"></a>**5** And it shall come to pass also that the remnants who are left of the land will marshal themselves, and shall become exceedingly angry, and shall vex the Gentiles with a sore vexation.

<a name="section-87_p6"></a>**6** And thus, with the sword and by bloodshed the inhabitants of the earth shall mourn; and with famine, and plague, and earthquake, and the thunder of heaven, and the fierce and vivid lightning also, shall the inhabitants of the earth be made to feel the wrath, and indignation, and chastening hand of an Almighty God, until the consumption decreed hath made a full end of all nations;

<a name="section-87_p7"></a>**7** That the cry of the saints, and of the blood of the saints, shall cease to come up into the ears of the Lord of Sabaoth, from the earth, to be avenged of their enemies.

<a name="section-87_p8"></a>**8** Wherefore, stand ye in holy places, and be not moved, until the day of the Lord come; for behold, it cometh quickly, saith the Lord. Amen.


---

## <a name="section-88"></a>Section 88

<a name="section-88_p1"></a>**1** Verily, thus saith the Lord unto you who have assembled yourselves together to receive his will concerning you:

<a name="section-88_p2"></a>**2** Behold, this is pleasing unto your Lord, and the angels rejoice over you; the alms of your prayers have come up into the ears of the Lord of Sabaoth, and are recorded in the book of the names of the sanctified, even them of the celestial world.

<a name="section-88_p3"></a>**3** Wherefore, I now send upon you another Comforter, even upon you my friends, that it may abide in your hearts, even the Holy Spirit of promise; which other Comforter is the same that I promised unto my disciples, as is recorded in the testimony of John.

<a name="section-88_p4"></a>**4** This Comforter is the promise which I give unto you of eternal life, even the glory of the celestial kingdom;

<a name="section-88_p5"></a>**5** Which glory is that of the church of the Firstborn, even of God, the holiest of all, through Jesus Christ his Son—

<a name="section-88_p6"></a>**6** He that ascended up on high, as also he descended below all things, in that he comprehended all things, that he might be in all and through all things, the light of truth;

<a name="section-88_p7"></a>**7** Which truth shineth. This is the light of Christ. As also he is in the sun, and the light of the sun, and the power thereof by which it was made.

<a name="section-88_p8"></a>**8** As also he is in the moon, and is the light of the moon, and the power thereof by which it was made;

<a name="section-88_p9"></a>**9** As also the light of the stars, and the power thereof by which they were made;

<a name="section-88_p10"></a>**10** And the earth also, and the power thereof, even the earth upon which you stand.

<a name="section-88_p11"></a>**11** And the light which shineth, which giveth you light, is through him who enlighteneth your eyes, which is the same light that quickeneth your understandings;

<a name="section-88_p12"></a>**12** Which light proceedeth forth from the presence of God to fill the immensity of space—

<a name="section-88_p13"></a>**13** The light which is in all things, which giveth life to all things, which is the law by which all things are governed, even the power of God who sitteth upon his throne, who is in the bosom of eternity, who is in the midst of all things.

<a name="section-88_p14"></a>**14** Now, verily I say unto you, that through the redemption which is made for you is brought to pass the resurrection from the dead.

<a name="section-88_p15"></a>**15** And the spirit and the body are the soul of man.

<a name="section-88_p16"></a>**16** And the resurrection from the dead is the redemption of the soul.

<a name="section-88_p17"></a>**17** And the redemption of the soul is through him that quickeneth all things, in whose bosom it is decreed that the poor and the meek of the earth shall inherit it.

<a name="section-88_p18"></a>**18** Therefore, it must needs be sanctified from all unrighteousness, that it may be prepared for the celestial glory;

<a name="section-88_p19"></a>**19** For after it hath filled the measure of its creation, it shall be crowned with glory, even with the presence of God the Father;

<a name="section-88_p20"></a>**20** That bodies who are of the celestial kingdom may possess it forever and ever; for, for this intent was it made and created, and for this intent are they sanctified.

<a name="section-88_p21"></a>**21** And they who are not sanctified through the law which I have given unto you, even the law of Christ, must inherit another kingdom, even that of a terrestrial kingdom, or that of a telestial kingdom.

<a name="section-88_p22"></a>**22** For he who is not able to abide the law of a celestial kingdom cannot abide a celestial glory.

<a name="section-88_p23"></a>**23** And he who cannot abide the law of a terrestrial kingdom cannot abide a terrestrial glory.

<a name="section-88_p24"></a>**24** And he who cannot abide the law of a telestial kingdom cannot abide a telestial glory; therefore he is not meet for a kingdom of glory. Therefore he must abide a kingdom which is not a kingdom of glory.

<a name="section-88_p25"></a>**25** And again, verily I say unto you, the earth abideth the law of a celestial kingdom, for it filleth the measure of its creation, and transgresseth not the law—

<a name="section-88_p26"></a>**26** Wherefore, it shall be sanctified; yea, notwithstanding it shall die, it shall be quickened again, and shall abide the power by which it is quickened, and the righteous shall inherit it.

<a name="section-88_p27"></a>**27** For notwithstanding they die, they also shall rise again, a spiritual body.

<a name="section-88_p28"></a>**28** They who are of a celestial spirit shall receive the same body which was a natural body; even ye shall receive your bodies, and your glory shall be that glory by which your bodies are quickened.

<a name="section-88_p29"></a>**29** Ye who are quickened by a portion of the celestial glory shall then receive of the same, even a fulness.

<a name="section-88_p30"></a>**30** And they who are quickened by a portion of the terrestrial glory shall then receive of the same, even a fulness.

<a name="section-88_p31"></a>**31** And also they who are quickened by a portion of the telestial glory shall then receive of the same, even a fulness.

<a name="section-88_p32"></a>**32** And they who remain shall also be quickened; nevertheless, they shall return again to their own place, to enjoy that which they are willing to receive, because they were not willing to enjoy that which they might have received.

<a name="section-88_p33"></a>**33** For what doth it profit a man if a gift is bestowed upon him, and he receive not the gift? Behold, he rejoices not in that which is given unto him, neither rejoices in him who is the giver of the gift.

<a name="section-88_p34"></a>**34** And again, verily I say unto you, that which is governed by law is also preserved by law and perfected and sanctified by the same.

<a name="section-88_p35"></a>**35** That which breaketh a law, and abideth not by law, but seeketh to become a law unto itself, and willeth to abide in sin, and altogether abideth in sin, cannot be sanctified by law, neither by mercy, justice, nor judgment. Therefore, they must remain filthy still.

<a name="section-88_p36"></a>**36** All kingdoms have a law given;

<a name="section-88_p37"></a>**37** And there are many kingdoms; for there is no space in the which there is no kingdom; and there is no kingdom in which there is no space, either a greater or a lesser kingdom.

<a name="section-88_p38"></a>**38** And unto every kingdom is given a law; and unto every law there are certain bounds also and conditions.

<a name="section-88_p39"></a>**39** All beings who abide not in those conditions are not justified.

<a name="section-88_p40"></a>**40** For intelligence cleaveth unto intelligence; wisdom receiveth wisdom; truth embraceth truth; virtue loveth virtue; light cleaveth unto light; mercy hath compassion on mercy and claimeth her own; justice continueth its course and claimeth its own; judgment goeth before the face of him who sitteth upon the throne and governeth and executeth all things.

<a name="section-88_p41"></a>**41** He comprehendeth all things, and all things are before him, and all things are round about him; and he is above all things, and in all things, and is through all things, and is round about all things; and all things are by him, and of him, even God, forever and ever.
